norman_crispin_06 = {
	name = Robert # Robert Crispin 'Phrangopoulos'
	dna = norman_crispin_06_robert_phrangopoulos
	dynasty = norman_crispin # Crispin
	culture = norman
	religion = catholic
	father = norman_crispin_01

	trait = education_martial_3

	# Personality Traits
	trait = brave
	trait = wrathful
	trait = greedy

	# Other Traits
	trait = reaver
	trait = lifestyle_traveler
	trait = aggressive_attacker

	disallow_random_traits = yes

	1040.1.1 = {
		birth = yes
	}
	1066.1.1 = {
		effect = {
			set_relation_best_friend = { reason = friend_generic_history target = character:34220 } # Roussel de Bailleul
			give_nickname = nick_phrangopoulos
			add_trait_xp = {
				trait = lifestyle_traveler
				track = travel
				value = { 45 55 }
			}
			add_trait_xp = {
				trait = lifestyle_traveler
				track = danger
				value = { 25 35 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dlc_feature = roads_to_power
				}
				change_government = landless_adventurer_government
				create_maa_regiment = {
					type = conrois
					size = 3
				}
			}
			add_character_flag = special_laamp_char
			add_character_flag = do_not_generate_starting_family
		}
	}
	1073.1.1 = {
		death = yes
	}
}
